<P STYLE="font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-
align: center"><B>NOTE REGARDING THIS FILING</B></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-
align: center"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-
align: justify; background-color: white">United American
Petroleum Corp. (the &ldquo;Registrant&rdquo;) is filing this Amendment on Form 
10-K/A (&ldquo;Amendment&rdquo;) to supplement
the Registrant&rsquo;s Annual Report on Form 10-K for the year ended December 
31, 2014, which the Registrant previously filed with
the&nbsp;Securities and Exchange Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;) on April 16, 
2015 (the &ldquo;Original Filing&rdquo;).</P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-
align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-
align: justify; background-color: white">The purpose
of this Amendment is to add the reserve report prepared by Mire &amp; 
Associates, Inc., which was inadvertently omitted from the
Original Filing due to an administrative oversight.</P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-
align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-
align: justify; background-color: white">No other changes
have been made to the Original Filing. This Amendment speaks as of the filing
date of the Original Filing, does not reflect events
that may have occurred subsequent to the date of the Original Filing, and does 
not modify or update in any way disclosures made
in the Original Filing. Accordingly, this Amendment should be read&nbsp;<FONT 
STYLE="background-color: white">in conjunction with
the Original Filing and our other filings made with the SEC subsequent to the 
filing of the Original Filing.&nbsp;</FONT><B>&nbsp;</B></P>
<P STYLE="font: 8pt/normal Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align:
justify">&nbsp;</P>

align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&nbsp;</P>

financial statements, and other financial information included in this report,

operations and cash flows of the registrant as of, and for, the periods
